Both the 101 and 405 freeways are only a couple of miles away via a quick commute on major (fast moving) streets, which is a major bonus. Olgitta &amp; Claude's home is neat &amp; clean, tastefully decorated, and very comfortable, warm, &amp; inviting. The guest bedroom has direct access to the kitchen and living room, and the queen size bed is very comfortable. There is plenty of parking available, and they are located in a nice neighborhood. Their baby (Max) is not only cute as a button, but he is very quiet too. The guest bedroom is on the opposite side of the house from the other bedrooms, so even if there was any noise (which there wasn't), you wouldn't hear it.                       <div data-reactid="1538">
                       Parks and recreation[edit] California State Parks operates the 5-acre (2.0 ha) Los Encinos State Historic Park in Encino.[15] The park includes the original nine-room de la Ossa Adobe, the Garnier Building, a blacksmith shop, a pond, and a natural spring.[16] The Sepulveda Dam Recreation Area, located in Encino,[17] includes the Woodley Worel/Magnus Cricket Complex with the four best grass cricket pitches in the United States. Host to many famous stars and games reflecting cricket's origins in Los Angeles from 1888.[18] Also included in the basin is the Encino Golf Course and the Balboa Golf Course, having a total of 36 golf holes. The Balboa Municipal Golf Course, a short-length golf course, was lengthened by Steve Timm in 2008. The Balboa course has a banquet room, back nine play, cart rental, club rental, classes, a lighted driving range, a lounge, practice chipping greens, practice putting greens, and a restaurant.[19] The Encino Municipal Golf Course, the second course of the two Sepulveda Dam courses, is a medium-length course that was designed by William P. Bell and Sons and opened in 1957. The course has large, tree-lined fairways. The course has the same features that the Balboa course has.[20] The Balboa Sports Complex in Encino includes a lighted baseball diamond, lighted outdoor basketball courts, a children's play area, a community room, a lighted football field, a lighted handball court, an indoor gymnasium without weights and with a capacity for 400 people, an unlighted soccer field, lighted tennis courts, and lighted volleyball courts.[21] The Sepulveda Basin Off-leash Dog Park is a dog park in Encino. The dog park has 6.5 acres (2.6 ha) of leash-free dog area, a 0.5-acre (0.20 ha) small dog area, an on-leash picnic area, 100 parking spots, and public telephones.[22] The Sepulveda Garden Center, a community garden area in Encino, has about 16 acres (6.5 ha) of land and 420 garden plots.[23]
